Danger and Rescue Efforts for the Jiangnan Seawall 68

The Provincial Government Decides to Allocate 100,000 Yuan for Rescue Expenses

Zhenjiang Dispatch: Regarding the Jiangnan Seawall, on the evening of the 26th, the Department of Construction received a telegram from Director Xue Zhaoshu of the seawall, stating that a violent wind and giant tide had destroyed more than a thousand zhang of the Bao Seawall, with dozens of breaches. In addition to the urgent blocking efforts, he requested to quickly bring funds for an on-site survey. The Water Conservancy Bureau, aware of the dangers to the dikes in Wuhan and Haining, Zhejiang, and because the autumn flood season had arrived, fearing unexpected events on the Jiangnan Seawall, advanced 5,000 yuan to the institute for emergency needs. Later, when a dangerous situation occurred, Director Mao led engineers with funds to conduct an on-site survey. After arriving, they reported in several telegrams that more than a thousand zhang of the Baoshan Seawall had been damaged, including more than 400 zhang of dangerous seawall, more than 40 zhang of gaps, and more than 30 zhang of breaches. Additionally, more than 290 zhang of iron-reinforced concrete stone slope at Beishidong and other places were completely destroyed. Thousands of piles along the seawall were broken. Efforts are being made to block the breaches, and more than 100,000 yuan is expected to be needed. The breach at Xuejiatan is the most dangerous. Materials are being prepared day and night to block it. More than 500 zhang of the Taicang Seawall were damaged, with 50 zhang of gaps and 40 zhang of breaches. The northern and southern ends of the cement wall section of the Daotang Temple were destroyed, and the body of the seawall in the northern section was completely collapsed and level with the ground, which is the most dangerous. All of the rescue projects carried out last month, except for the wooden piles, were also destroyed. Efforts are being made to block all the breaches, and the estimated cost is 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. In addition to the 30,000 yuan already advanced by the Department of Construction, the Water Conservancy Bureau was also ordered to send additional engineers, and the magistrates of Taicang and Baoshan were telegraphed to hire laborers. The directors of the construction bureaus of the two counties, along with technicians, went to assist. A proposal was submitted to the Provincial Government meeting to quickly allocate 100,000 yuan from the provincial treasury for important projects, which was approved by yesterday's Provincial Committee meeting. Several places in the Songjiang Seawall were also damaged, and the Department is sending personnel to investigate.

Ye and Zhang Arrive in Shao and Gao to Survey the Disaster 69

Yangzhou Dispatch: The visits from Provincial Chairman Ye Chucang of Jiangsu to the disaster areas of Shao and You have been reported in detail in previous news. On the morning of August 31st, at 9:00 AM, Ye Chucang took the Yuan Chang special ship from Zhenjiang, passing Yangzhou, escorted by the Jialu warship. Those who traveled with him included Wu Tongju, the director of the Grand Canal Engineering Office, Cheng Yiqing, a standing member of the Relief Association, and Chen Zhao, the magistrate of Jiangdu County. At 11:00 AM, the ship arrived at Shaobo, and he immediately disembarked to inspect the dike for a week. Then he returned to the ship and sailed upstream. Li Mingyang, the director of the Provincial Security Office, heard that Ye and others were heading north, so he immediately invited Wang Shuxiang, who was experienced in managing the canal (Wang was a former counselor of the Grand Canal Engineering Office), to take the Gao special ship south. He met Ye at Lujin. Li and Wang Shuxiang boarded the ship to pay their respects, and they discussed the restoration of the river dike and all measures to prevent the collapse of other banks on the ship. At 7:00 PM, the ship docked at the dike on the north gate of Gaoyou, which was in a vast expanse of water. He stayed overnight. The next morning, he traveled north from You. It is said that this inspection will end at Qingjiangpu. After Zhang Zhijiang, the supervisor, learned of the Grand Canal breach, he returned to Yangzhou from Beijing a few days ago. In addition to purchasing dry food and sending personnel to the disaster areas to rescue more than a thousand disaster victims, on August 31st, he and Secretary-General Sun Yucheng, Adjutant Song Bangrong, Counselor Wang Chunru, and more than 60 guards rented a small steamer from the Tiantai Merchant Shipping Bureau, two tugboats, a civilian boat, and two other boats, loaded with more than 500 bags of dry food, and headed to the Shaogao area to rescue the disaster victims. At 8:20 AM, the ship arrived at Shaobo. He saw that fewer houses had collapsed in the south of the street, the loss in the middle city was heavier, and the entire north city had disintegrated. The water in the street was the same as the river. According to statistics, more than half of the houses in the town had collapsed. There were a total of 21 breaches, large and small, of which 9 had been blocked. In addition to distributing some of the dry food, Zhang also instructed the troops stationed in the town to work hard to help repair and rob. At 9:10 AM, he left Shao and headed north. Because the water in the Grand Canal was unusually turbulent, fearing that it would enter the breach, he slowly advanced northeast along the lake. Along the way, except for occasionally seeing the treetops slightly exposed to the water, knowing that it was land, everything else was a vast expanse of water. At 2:00 PM, he arrived in Gaoyou and ascended the city from the city wall that had been excavated. The inside of the city was like a crystal palace. All the disaster victims were sitting on the top of the city wall, living in thatched sheds. The sad and tragic scene cannot be described in words. The magistrate of the county, Wang Long, cried bitterly when he saw Zhang, and Zhang also shed tears. At the moment, the county government is temporarily moved to the Guandi Temple outside the South Gate (the entire city has a higher terrain in the South Gate and less water). The Public Security Bureau is located in a tea house, and the Finance Bureau has no funds to collect. Education and construction have been suspended long ago. Zhang distributed all the dry food he brought. He spent the night on the boat in Gaoyou and discussed with Chairman Ye the two key points of short-term and long-term solutions. The short-term solution is to block the breach, and the long-term solution is to consolidate the river dike. At dawn on the first day, after Ye Qiding headed north, Zhang drummed the wheels and returned south. (September 2nd)

Disaster Relief and Aftermath in Shao and Gao 70

Eight Counties Including Jiangtai Petition for Urgent Blocking of Breaches

Yangzhou Dispatch: The disaster victims and relief efforts in Shao and You have been detailed in previous reports. It is now known that in Taixian, after the Shaobo dike breached, the east, west, and north townships were all submerged. Except for the South Gate, the rest of the city became a swamp. The special commissioner of the county party headquarters took a Jiang steamer to Yangzhou on the first day to report the disaster and arrange relief work. Chairman Ye, who went north to survey the disaster on August 31st, arrived here at noon on the first day, docked outside Fuyun Gate, entered the city to discuss official business, and returned to the original boat to return to the province. All the refugees who have been rescued, in addition to the Jiangdu Emergency Relief Association, the Red Swastika Society, and the Supervisor's Office, have been transported to Yangzhou in turn, handed over to the reception center, or escorted across the river. On the first day, Xu Guocun, the leader of the second team of the Jiangbei Disaster Relief and Relief Association of Zhenjiang, transported more than 400 refugees from the Shaoyou area, leaving more than 200 people and sending them to the Changsheng Temple reception center, and sending the rest to the Zhenjiang reception center. Jing Mingming, Xu Baoheng, and Wu Jinren of Hejia Lane, South Gate, went to distribute relief, 300 articles per person, and then went to the Putuo Temple reception center (which originally had 47 refugees) to distribute the same amount. The relief goods received by the Emergency Relief Association today (the first day), in addition to sporadic dry food and relief money, the largest was Wang Bailing's aid of 1,000 foreign yuan and the philanthropist Wei Cufan's 200,000 articles. In addition to sending personnel to transport a large amount of dry food to various disaster areas for distribution, the association also hired 70 officials, gentry, wealthy merchants, and financiers from the Jiangdu Chamber of Commerce, together with the chambers of commerce of Taigao, Xingbao, Yanfu, and other eight counties, to present a joint petition to the National Government and the Provincial Government's Huai River Guidance Committee, stating that disaster relief and blocking the breaches should be equally emphasized, and planned six measures for execution. In addition, Fang Yaoxi and others from Jiangzhou have been sent to the city to report the disaster and ask for relief, roughly saying that there are more than 10,000 refugees waiting for relief urgently, and if they are delayed, they will freeze to death. As for the water situation, the water level of the canal outside the city fell slightly yesterday, but this afternoon the east wind was strong again, and the tide was supporting it, and it increased by a foot again. The dikes and weirs of the various islands near the river, which were spared before, are in imminent danger again. All the floating corpses in the river have been transported in coffins by the emergency relief association and the Red Swastika Society, and handed over to those responsible for collecting the corpses for collection and burial. However, it is a pity that there are many corpses and few coffins, and omissions are still unavoidable. (September 1st)

Central Disaster Survey Team Arrives in Anhui 71

More Than a Thousand Floating Corpses in Wuhu Cannot Be Buried

Wuhu Dispatch: The flood disaster in Anhui Province is so severe that it is unprecedented in nearly a century. Unexpectedly, a hurricane struck again the day before yesterday, and more than a thousand refugees were swept into the flood by the wind and waves. Other losses are even more unspeakable. At the moment, the corpses are scattered and drifting downstream, accumulating on Xiliang Mountain, reaching more than 600 bodies. Those that have not drifted away are mostly connected in series with ropes and tied to large trees, such as Xingchun and Shouchun dikes, which are everywhere. Although charitable organizations have prepared many coffins for burial, there is also a sigh of too many corpses and too few coffins. Now, in addition to carrying a large amount of steamed buns and distributing them every day, emergency relief agencies have also set up clinics to prevent epidemics. Qian Danwu, a member of the Central Disaster Inspection Committee, and Wen Yi, a member of the Provincial Department of Construction, came to Wuhu from the province yesterday and went to the county government to discuss the joint disaster inspection method with Magistrate Yu. That night, the Flood Relief Association and the Wufan Five Counties Relief Association negotiated with Qian to hire a special ship at 8:00 AM this morning (the 31st) to conduct an on-site inspection of the disaster areas such as Mapu, Bajiaodian, and Fenglinwei along the West River. It is planned to rush back tonight and collect disaster area photos, investigation forms, and solicit opinions from all parties on water conservancy dredging and other matters tomorrow (the 1st) in Wuhu. On the 2nd, they will go to Fanchang, Nanling, Xuancheng, and other counties, and return to Wuhu around September 17th, and then go to Dangtu for inspection. It is expected to return to Beijing on the 19th and transfer to Guoyang, Lingbi, and Mengcheng to inspect the disaster situation. As for Zhuang Yan, the commissioner sent by the central government with 170,000 yuan for relief, he needs to wait for the completion of the five-member disaster investigation group before he can allocate the relief money according to the severity of the disaster. The Wufan Five Counties Relief Association previously sent Zhai Zhancheng as a representative to Beijing and Shanghai to raise relief funds. Although they have raised 40,000 yuan in relief funds and 2,000 bags of flour, they cannot be transported to Wuhu for a while, which is a concern that distant water cannot put out a nearby fire. Therefore, the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce issued a circular today, calling for urgent relief. The water level has been rising steadily for days, and people are becoming more panicked. The customs water level has reached more than three zhang and eight inches! (August 31st)

The Yellow River Water Level is No Longer a Concern 72

The Water Level is Equal to the Pre-Flood Level

But There Are Small Waves in the Liugong Section Upstream

Jinan Dispatch: The Yellow River water level has been decreasing day by day, and the water from Shaanxi Province upstream has gradually reached Shandong Province. The water level is stable, and there is no danger. This morning (the 31st), the River Affairs Bureau received a water report from Shaanxi, stating that the river water has dropped by eight inches and six points compared to three days ago. According to the Luokou water report, the river water has dropped by six inches today, and the water level is eight zhang seven chi and three cun. Based on the current water level, it is equal to the water level before the flood. Only the Liugong section (Liuyuan) in the upstream section has small waves due to the narrower riverbed. Each dam is inevitably damaged by the rushing torrents. The River Affairs Bureau received an urgent telegram from Liugong at 2:30 PM today (the 31st), which said: The water rose nine inches this morning, and the current is retreating, hitting dams 14, 15, 16, and 17. A section of the newly made sweep dam at the 16th dam is isolated and helpless, and the upper corner has been steeply eroded by three chi. The two dams at the 17th dam are low above the water. Although a section of the cross-ear dam has been added to the upper end of the No. 1 sweep dam, the waves are surging and extremely turbulent, and it is feared that it will be difficult to resist. Furthermore, there is a shortage of materials, which is very difficult. In addition to urging Magistrate Li of Pu County to send police to the countryside to rush and urge the transportation of straw materials to meet the urgent needs, I hereby report to you. Xu Desheng, Section Chief, kowtows. (August 31st)

Record of Inspection of the Flood Disaster at Weishan Lake in Xuzhou 73

The North of Xuzhou City Has Been Submerged

Xuzhou Correspondence: Weishan Lake in the north of Xuzhou is connected to Nanyang Lake in southern Shandong. It collects water from the Grand Canal and has dams for storage and discharge. The water discharged from the south bank flows south through Lanjia Mountain to Wanzhai, twelve li north of Xuzhou City, then turns east into the Jing River, which is the largest construction in Xuzhou, the Jing Mountain Bridge. This summer, there was heavy rain in Xuzhou, and the water in the old course of the Yellow River rose sharply. However, Weishan Lake has not yet overflowed, as the water from the old course of the Yellow River and the water discharged from the south of Weishan Lake are not connected at all. Recently, the water danger in Xuzhou City has passed, but heavy rains in southern Shandong caused mountain floods to break out, and the water in Nanyang Lake overflowed and flooded the south. At the same time, the water in Weishan Lake rose sharply, and the villages along the lake became a watery realm. Local authorities reported the disaster to the county government one after another. The Water Disaster Relief Association, considering that the water discharged from the south of Weishan Lake was very close to the city, specially sent Hu Yunqing from the Agricultural Rehabilitation Committee, Wang Yongfu from the Construction Bureau, and Li Yuhai from the Red Cross Society to inspect on August 29. That morning, they departed from Xuzhou City by rickshaw, passing through Pingyamenkou, Xiaogushan, Shitun, Tanggou, and Taoyuan. The low-lying areas along the way were all flooded, and there was no hope for the autumn harvest. In the afternoon, they arrived at Zhengji, forty li north of Xuzhou, which is very close to the lake. The area north of the market town, being low-lying, was already submerged, and the disaster was severe. On the morning of the 30th, they traveled fifteen li east from Zhengji to Wanglou by the lake, and then changed to a boat to sail southeast along Liuzhuang, Dingji, Taikeng, Wangtang, Ronggou, Sunzhuang, Donglou, Qianhou Gaotan, Daxiao Yanzhuang, Xia Zhoulou, Qinlou, Wafang, and other places. It was a vast expanse of water, with only the ridges and eaves of houses exposed, spanning more than twenty li in width and length. The number of people who died in the water must be countless. The boat landed at Weizhuang and turned to Dachacheng along the Xinyan. Dachacheng was the ancient state of Chonghouhu, and the terrain was relatively high. The overflowing water of Weishan Lake had reached the Grandma Temple north of Dachacheng, and Dachacheng was only thirty li away from the city. Traveling southeast from Dachacheng to Wanzhai River, the river connected to Weishan Lake, and the water had already reached the shore. About two li from Wanzhai, there was the Checun Kou Dam, which was the first embankment to protect the city from flooding. Unfortunately, it had fallen into disrepair and was breached in many places. The water nearby had already submerged the shins. Then, they returned to Xuzhou City from Machang Lake, and it was already dusk. It was found that the first line of defense in Xuzhou against the water of Weishan Lake was the Checun Kou Dam, and the second was the levee north of Bazijie. Since the Checun Kou Dam had fallen into disrepair, the water flowed from there into Machang Lake north of Bazijie, and the rice fields were about to be completely flooded. Fortunately, the levee north of Bazijie prevented this, so the city was still not in danger, but the villages north of the city were already in a dire situation. According to statistics, the lake water rose south, overflowing the original bank by fifteen li, rising southeast to Dachacheng, southwest to Wanglou, and directly south to Hukeng. The deep areas were about seven or eight chi deep, where double-awning masts could sail, and the shallow areas were also three or four chi deep. Fields and houses spanning more than twenty li east and west were all flooded, and the disaster was severe. Therefore, relief efforts cannot be delayed. (One Day)

Long-Distance Call Between Guangzhou and Hong Kong 74

Telephone Ceremony Held on September 1st

Hong Kong Correspondence: The long-distance telephone between Guangzhou and Hong Kong was officially opened on the first of this month. First, Lin Yun'kai of the Guangdong Provincial Government and Governor Peel of Hong Kong exchanged congratulatory messages on the phone, followed by celebrations in Guangzhou and Hong Kong. The Guangzhou side held the ceremony at the Provincial Government, with attendees including the Chairman of the Provincial Government, the Mayor of Guangzhou, and representatives of various consulates. The Hong Kong side held the ceremony at the Hong Kong Telephone Company, with attendees including the Governor of Hong Kong, members of the Municipal Council, members of the Chamber of Commerce, the President of HSBC Bank, and representatives of various newspapers. This event was jointly organized by the Guangdong Provincial Government and the Hong Kong Telephone Company, requiring an estimated expenditure of over three million yuan. The telephone line was installed along the Kowloon-Canton Railway, approximately one hundred and fifty miles long, using the latest type of armored cable, manufactured by the London Standard Telephone & Cables Company. The China General Edison Company on Jiangxi Road, Shanghai, is its liaison company. The telephone can simultaneously connect to thirty locations. Guangzhou telephone users must deposit thirty yuan before they can make calls to Hong Kong, with a charge of two yuan and seven jiao per three minutes. As business between Guangzhou and Hong Kong is known to be booming, this line will greatly benefit commerce in both places.

Local Correspondence

Jiading 75

Removal of the Chief of the Public Security Bureau. The County Chief of the Public Security Bureau, Zhu Shou, was recently suspected of being heavily involved in a case where police officers extorted a large sum of money from a Mr. Bai in the Northern Township. County Magistrate Pan not only suspended Zhu from his duties and detained him at the county government for a thorough investigation, but also reported the matter to the provincial department. The provincial government has decided to remove Zhu from his post and investigate. The vacancy has been filled by transferring Shen Jinghua, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau of Qingpu County, to Jiading.

Suzhou 76

The Appeal Hearing of the Guan Daming Rape Case. The Story of the Remarkable Shanghai Woman Zheng Xuanying, Sister of Zheng Ying, Who Was Rescued After Attempting Suicide in the Huangpu River, and Accused Guan Daming, the Manager of the Gaultier Shoe Store at 152 Jing'an Temple Road, Shanghai, of Rape, and Attached a Private Suit Seeking Compensation of 20,000 Yuan. After the Shanghai District Court ruled that Guan Daming was guilty of raping a woman under the age of twenty, and sentenced him to three years and six months of imprisonment, Guan refused to accept the ruling and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Suzhou Higher Court. Yesterday (the 2nd) morning, the presiding judge of the Second Criminal Division, Li Mian, opened the court to try Guan. Those who were summoned to court included the appellant Zheng Xuanying, Zheng's father Youhe, Meng Baosong, the accountant of the Xingaosheng Hotel, the waiter Wu Ronglin, and the original lawyers Wei Wenhan and Zhan Jifeng, and the lawyer Cao Lin, who handled the private suit for the appellant. First, Guan Daming was questioned. According to his testimony, the Qiuqin (i.e., Zheng Ying) sisters borrowed a house from me in March of last year and lived on the third floor. I was the sub-landlord, and the second floor of the store was occupied by outsiders. Because the Zheng sisters often used the front door when entering and exiting, I intervened, and they resented me for it and falsely accused me of rape. Next, Zheng Xuanying testified that she was seventeen years old, studying at Peide Elementary School, and her sister Qiuqin worked at the Shenghuo Newspaper Office. There were five people in her family, including her parents and a younger brother. Guan Daming was the sub-landlord, and we used the back door when entering and exiting. We did not have any quarrels with Guan. In June of last year, Guan first invited me to see a movie at the Da Guangming Cinema. On October 18th, he took me to Room 30 of the Xingaosheng Hotel on Wuma Road. Once, he opened a room at the Shenzhou Hotel at 204 Sima Road. The judge asked what we did when we opened the room. Xuanying blushed and did not speak, and began to cry softly. The judge then announced a temporary ban on public attendance. It was heard that Zheng Xuanying testified at the time that she had been raped twice. Later, she met her father on Gordon Road, who saw her riding in Guan Daming's chartered car, so he drove her out of the house after returning home. She then ran away on December 26th and lived in the home of Cai Yueying, a young woman on Carter Road, until she was rescued after attempting suicide in the Huangpu River on June 13th of this year. She is currently living at the home of Lawyer Cao. Then, the witness Meng Baosong testified that on the 18th day of the tenth lunar month last year, a man and a woman opened Room 30, and they left after only two hours. At that time, there was a business card with the words "Gaultier Shoe Store" printed on it. On the seventh day of the twelfth lunar month, she came again and opened Room 26, but it was only the woman alone. The traveler's single slip was written as Guan Daming, and she stayed for two days before leaving. The woman was indeed Zheng Xuanying. After the interrogation, the judge instructed that more witnesses should be summoned in this case, and a hearing would be scheduled again after further review.

Two People Drowned After a Brick Boat Was Hit. Cha Genggeng, a 26-year-old from Changshu, his wife Zhang, and his daughter Zhaoyuan, who was only two years old, loaded a boat with bricks and tiles from Xiaobaimi, Changshu, a few days ago, and went to Ma Shengtai outside Xumen, Suzhou, to unload the goods. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday (the 1st), at 7:00 p.m., the boat arrived at the Dahui Bridge. In front of them was Zhou Genrong's coal boat. Because the boat was too heavy and the current was too strong, it could not move forward and instead retreated, causing the stern of the boat to hit the bow of the brick boat. The boat immediately shattered and sank. Cha and his wife and daughter all fell into the water. The Third District Water Police and the Water Patrol Team tried to rescue them. Only Cha Genggeng was rescued, and his wife and daughter were washed away by the waves and could not be found. Yesterday (the 2nd) afternoon, at 4:00 p.m., the body of Cha's wife, Zhang, was found near Dahui. The coal boat that caused the accident has been detained by the police station, and the perpetrator is being investigated.

The Chamber of Commerce has received donations of nearly a thousand yuan in one or two days. The county party headquarters also held an executive committee meeting yesterday (the 1st) to decide on measures for flood donation and issued a special issue on the flood to promote awareness.

Notorious Bandit Qin Ergou and Others Executed by Firing Squad. Notorious bandit Qin Ergou was an accomplice of the bandit leader Gao Xiaosheng. After Gao Xiaosheng was executed, Qin hid at sea and secretly returned to Changzhou from time to time to carry out activities. Recently, he was arrested in Shanghai by detectives sent by the county government. After being escorted to Changzhou, he confessed to various cases of kidnapping, ransom, and robbery without denial. Director Zhang, who was also the Director of the Local Clearance Bureau, immediately sentenced Qin and six other recently captured bandits, including Sheng Badu, Ji Binggen, Qian Fugeng, Jiang Xiqing, Jiang Maogan, and Jiang Bingsheng, to death and submitted the sentences to the provincial government for approval. At 6:00 a.m. on the 2nd, the police escorted Qin and the other seven to the execution ground, verified their identities, and executed them by firing squad.

Zhenjiang 78

Guo Yanmo Sent to Prison to Serve His Sentence. Guo Yanmo, the former manager of the Zhenjiang branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was sued by an employee, Ran Shaohua, for smoking opium. After two trials, he was sentenced to two months of imprisonment and a fine of one thousand yuan. The sentence was finalized long ago, but Guo had not reported to the authorities. Multiple warrants were issued to his guarantors to compel him to surrender. He was released on bail again. It is now known that Guo was found by his guarantors yesterday afternoon and escorted to the court to request the withdrawal of the bail and request immediate execution of the sentence. Prosecutor Li opened the court, questioned him, and immediately ordered him to be detained pending execution. His wife, Zhang, was arrested and executed last month and had completed her sentence yesterday. The elderly couple met in the waiting room, and their situation was very tragic.

Wang Yuanchen Filed for Retrial. Yi Ruichang sued Wang Yuanchen for negligent injury. Jiangyin 79

The Jiangyin Regiment Police Were Arrested for Disregarding Human Life. On August 1st, Zhou Dougen from Zhuxiang, Zhouzhuang, was reported by Gu Zigen to capture Zhang Guangde (Nantuan Regiment Chief) from Zhang Deyuan's noodle shop in Houcheng and sent him to the Eighth District Office. Upon receiving the report, the Houcheng Business Regiment and the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, led by instructor Wu Kuan and Branch Chief Zhang Ke, went to rescue him, resulting in a conflict with the farmers there. (The Houcheng side referred to them as the Big Sword Society, while the Zhouzhuang side claimed they were only a self-defense group.) Instructor Wu Kuan ordered the firing of guns, killing Zhou Dougen and drowning Ding Zhuoan and Xu Bingxiang. After the official authorities examined the bodies, they summoned a thousand witnesses to investigate the case once. Yesterday (the 1st), they conducted interrogations for the first and second times. Peng County Magistrate interrogated Zhou Jiangshi, the wife of the deceased Zhou Dougen, and more than 20 witnesses including Zhou Yu'an and Zhou Huangniu. As a result of the interrogation, it was determined that the Business Regiment and the Public Security Bureau were both responsible for protecting the local people and could not treat them as enemies. Wu Kuan's statement that he fired more than sixty shots into the sky did not match the gunshot wounds on the bodies of the deceased, which was obviously an excuse and disregard for human life. He was ordered to be detained in the confinement room. Zhang Shouchang and Cao Guanghua, squad leaders of the Business Regiment, were detained in the guardhouse. Zhang Ke was released on bail from two shops, and the others were ordered to return.

Rugao 81

The Red Bandits of Daxizhuang Were Completely Eliminated. Rugao's notorious bandit Yu Xian (also known as Yu Xiawan) sneaked back to carry out activities. In the past, he killed more than a dozen villagers in Xiwuzhuang and other places. The main culprit has not yet been arrested. On the 28th, Yu led more than a dozen bandits to ambush at the home of Miao Yuansheng in Daxizhuang, preparing to kill and set fires at night. Unexpectedly, Yang, the squad leader of the first squad of the first detachment of the county police, learned of this and immediately dispatched more than 20 soldiers to search and suppress them. At the same time, he informed Chen, the detachment leader, to dispatch more than 20 soldiers, as well as Li, the squad leader of Taixing, and Sun, the head of the Luhong Security Regiment, to surround the area on all sides. The bandits opened fire and resisted stubbornly, while lying in ambush inside the Miao residence, refusing to come out. The soldiers, seeing that the bandits were numerous, had many guns, and were hiding inside the house, had no way to attack. They devised a plan to set the house on fire, so that the bandits had nowhere to hide. When the bandits saw the fire, they fired fiercely, while still trying to break out. In the end, all the bandits hiding in the Miao residence were killed one by one. The notorious bandit Yu Xian was killed while trying to escape outside the Miao residence. Yesterday (the 29th), squad leader Yang transported Yu's corpse and two other bandit heads to the city and reported the situation to County Magistrate Qian. After being confirmed by Zhu Quan, the district chief of Zhentao, that it was indeed the notorious bandit Yu Xian, they were displayed in front of the Guan Yue Temple for public viewing.

However, the terrain there is treacherous, making it difficult to suppress. Four soldiers were killed by bullets and several soldiers were wounded. The battalion commander was furious upon hearing the news and has been mobilizing large forces to continue the suppression in order to eliminate the banditry.

The Ministry of Education Promulgates Regulations on Reviewing Party Ideology Teachers 85

The Ministry of Education, upon the order of the Executive Yuan, forwarded the Provisional Regulations on Reviewing Party Ideology Teachers and the Organizational Rules for the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers, issuing a circular to all national colleges and universities and provincial and municipal education departments, stating: "Based on Executive Yuan Order No. 4242, the following is to be implemented. Based on National Government Civil Service Office Document No. 6701, the Central Executive Committee's Document No. 715 forwards the Provisional Regulations on Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers and the Organizational Rules for the Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers. Since their implementation, based on the actual situation, there are still some points that are not entirely appropriate. After revisions, please inform your subordinate competent authorities. The Chairman has instructed that the matter be forwarded for notification. This case was previously submitted to the Executive Yuan through Central Executive Committee Document No. 1365, and a reply was approved, instructing the Ministry of Education to comply. Now, based on the aforementioned reasons, in addition to replying, the original documents are enclosed for your review and implementation." Accordingly, the original document is copied and issued, instructing you to notify and instruct your subordinates to notify accordingly. This order. (Regulations and rules are temporarily omitted)

The Ministry of Education Orders the Prohibition of the Commercial Press From Selling Sanmin Zhuyi Textbooks 86

Schools Are Not Allowed to Use Unrevised Versions

The Ministry of Education has approved a letter from the Central Training Department stating that the New Era Sanmin Zhuyi Textbook published by the Commercial Press is prohibited from being used before it is revised. A circular was issued to the education departments of all provinces and cities, stating: "The revised version of the New Era Sanmin Zhuyi Textbook for junior high schools submitted by the Commercial Press for review has been preliminarily reviewed by this Ministry. As it concerns party ideology, the original book and the preliminary review notes have been sent to the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee for review. The reply states that the book has many shortcomings and numerous errors, and should be greatly revised and resubmitted for review. Before this book is revised, the published versions should be inspected by party departments at all levels at local bookstores and schools, and the Commercial Press should be instructed not to sell them. At the same time, the education administrative organs of all provinces and cities should be instructed to direct all secondary schools not to use them. Accordingly, the review opinions are enclosed along with the original book for your information and action." The original book and review opinions have been sent to the Ministry. In addition to ordering the Commercial Press to comply and issuing separate orders, you are hereby ordered to instruct all secondary schools under your jurisdiction not to use the book before it is revised. This order.

Local News

The Municipal Education Bureau Announces That Staff Members Should Carry Credentials When Inspecting Private Schools 87

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announces that all staff members of the Bureau should carry their staff identification cards when inspecting private schools. Announcement No. 46 states: "Recently, it has been discovered that unscrupulous individuals are impersonating staff members of this Bureau to conduct investigations at private schools in this city, which is extremely audacious and hateful. Staff members of this Bureau have always been provided with staff identification cards. In the future, when this Bureau sends staff members to inspect or investigate private schools, the staff members will first present their staff identification cards as proof. If the inspectors or investigators do not have staff identification cards from this Bureau, the school may immediately send them to the Public Security Bureau to be dealt with according to the law and report the details of the incident in detail for verification and handling." This announcement is hereby made known to all. September 2, 20th year of the Republic of China.

Charity Basketball Game: Chizhi vs. Xiqing 92

Scheduled for August 8th and 10th

In addition to holding charity football matches, the Chinese National Sports Association has also invited the Chizhi University basketball team, the Jiangda Basketball Championship team, and the Xiqing team, the Shanghai basketball champion team, to hold charity games at the Chinese Basketball Hall at 7:30 p.m. on the 8th and 10th of this month. Second Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament 101

China Retains Championship

Japan Too Depressed, Forfeits Last Two Matches

China Wins 4-1 Today Without Effort

The second Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament, with participants from six countries—China, England, Portugal, America, Canada, and Japan—has been underway since its opening on the 15th. After a series of eliminations, the final was contested by China and Japan. Two matches had already been played, with each side winning one. China won the doubles match, and the remaining two singles matches were Qiu Feihai against Machida and Jiang Daozhang against Hyosaku Tawara. These were originally scheduled to be played at 4:30 PM today. Yesterday afternoon, the Japanese sports authorities notified the Association, stating that both singles matches would be forfeited. Therefore, China won 4-1 without effort, defeating Japan to win this year's championship and retain the honor.

Jiangsu Education Department Refuses Athletes from Jing and Hu to Participate in Preliminary Selections 106

One: To Take Away the Opportunities of Jiangsu People

Two: It Would Be Unseemly for Both Parties

Mr. Wu Bangwei, the director of the Zhenjiang Public Sports Field in Jiangsu Province, came to Shanghai yesterday on official business. He made the following statement to reporters: For this National Games Jiangsu preliminary selection, the Education Department stipulated that only athletes within the scope of Jiangsu Province are allowed to participate. The entire team or individual athletes from Nanjing and Shanghai are uniformly rejected from registration. First, to take away the opportunities of Jiangsu Province athletes, and second, it would be unseemly for both parties. Jiangsu's sports results are certainly lagging behind, but if we rely on other units to slightly compete for a position in the National Games, then the glory gained would be dishonorable. Moreover, accepting athletes from outside the province would foster arrogance among athletes, making it even more unworthy.

Cotton Market Stability 115

The cotton market is stable, but the conditions for American and Indian cotton remain pessimistic. Therefore, various foreign firms are competitively selling foreign cotton in the market, seeking a way out due to excessive inventory. As a result, prices are quite low, and factories are purchasing a significant amount of Rangoon cotton. Consequently, large players are actively selling off their holdings. However, the majority of local cotton merchants are leaning towards a bullish outlook, as the cotton fields in Hankou have suffered severe damage from floods, and the inventory of old cotton is low. Although the selling price of foreign cotton is low, it cannot reach Shanghai in time. The price of gold is also firm, and the outstanding debt is too large, with many non-industry players selling short. It will be difficult to avoid being squeezed later. Therefore, the volume sold off by large players in recent days has been almost entirely absorbed by their peers, and the situation can still be maintained. In summary, the depression in the global cotton industry has a significant impact.

▲ Hankou Standard Leveling: The Hankou standard pre-market opened with a slight drop in American cotton, softening market sentiment. Although there were large players, there were also many buyers. Grain, Ye Xie, Nanqiao New Japonica Rice on the Market 120

▲ In Nanshi Ye Shu Nanqiao, new japonica rice has been loaded onto ships, amounting to 200 shi. The quality of the rice is good, and the initial price is 15 yuan and 3 jiao. However, there are some urban-rural transactions involving old goods. Due to the obscure weather, fresh goods are still in demand, but the supply of medium-grade goods is sluggish. After the price increases, the market is stable. Although early and late rice have weakened slightly, local buyers are picking fresh goods and advancing prices slightly. The new japonica rice goods are still sporadic, and higher-quality ones are still available, while lower-quality ones are normal. The prices of Yanglu tip and Biantou are fixed tightly.

▲ The market in Xin Zha hasn't been able to turn around. There are not many people at the market in the morning, and appetite is low. Thick japonica rice continues to tighten by one jiao. People are losing interest. New japonica rice and early and late rice opened at a settled price. Yanglu tip and Butip are out of stock, and prices have also increased by about one jiao. Transactions of No. 1 and No. 2 Biantou are becoming more active. Kunshan rice is not selling well, and prices continue to fall. Foreign rice spot sales are sluggish, and customer assistance is stagnant. The situation is mediocre. The supply from the west is still surging, with about 323,300 shi of various goods from river factories being sold.

50,000 Bags of Foreign Rice Newly Arrived 121

Market price drops by 3-4 jiao.

Yesterday's foreign rice market conditions: Spot prices fell by 3-4 jiao. Only then did Benjie sell 450 bags of Qieladi, priced at only 13 yuan and 3 jiao. A small amount of 200 tons of recycled Jiaoxiao was sold, also down by 30%. Yesterday's price decline was mainly due to a new batch of foreign rice arriving, totaling 50,000 bags, loaded by Renji Bingchang, etc. Although they were displayed on the market, no one inquired about them. Moreover, there are still large orders scheduled to arrive in the coming days. It is said that a total of more than 200,000 bags will arrive this month. The local appetite for Taizhou rice is very good, and the market is also firm. 100 bags of Taizhou white rice were offered at 13 yuan and 1 jiao, and 500 bags of rice were offered at 11 yuan and 2 jiao. The quality of the goods is better, and the price is also higher than the previous market.

Flour Market Turns Attractive 122

After the opening in the morning and afternoon, the flour market gradually showed a stable and attractive situation. Although actual sales were not moving and transactions were not smooth, some people believe that the 1,500 bushels of US wheat for disaster relief reported may be suspended due to unresolved conditions. If it cannot be determined, then the digestion of Shanghai's inventory will inevitably surge. Therefore, some floating longs are taking advantage of the trend to absorb them. Although transactions are not strong, the market sentiment is gradually rising. However, based on the speculation of the wheat market abroad, it is still in surplus. In any case, the Shanghai market should have little fear of shortages. As a result, this month is up 1 fen and 2.5 li compared to the previous day, October is up 1 fen, November is up 1 fen and 2.5 li, December is up 1.5 fen, and February is up 1 fen.

Wheat Futures Seemingly in a Stable Situation 123

After the opening in the morning and afternoon, the wheat market seemed to turn stable. Although the quoted prices of foreign wheat did not change much, the US wheat borrowed by the government from the United States was currently suspended because the two sides had not fully agreed. People inside and outside the port inevitably worried about this. There were few sell-offs, and buyers were still sufficient to support the market. Therefore, near and far terms have all improved. However, according to the speculation of the general public, this disaster relief wheat will eventually be realized sooner or later. As a result, September and October each rose 3 fen from the previous day, November rose 2 fen, and December to February each rose 3 fen. The spot wheat market situation remains stagnant, with few transactions. Six-Hop wheat was offered at 3 taels, 7 qian, and 1 fen, and Double Phoenix wheat was offered at 3 taels, 7 qian, and 2 fen, totaling 700 bags, which were handled by Fuxin.

Sugar Market Limited Trading, Quiet Inflow and Outflow 124

Coarse Sand White Dumping Falls Further

Yesterday's sugar market area telegram: The price of Cuban spot sugar is 1.375, down 3125 from the previous telegram. New York sugar futures for September are 1.32, December is 1.30, March next year is 1.34, and May is 1.39, with only May falling by 1 fen from before, and the other months unchanged. The association's trading was very quiet. Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand white new goods were 11 taels and 7 qian, and old goods in white bags were 11 taels and 6 qian. No. 20 medium sand white was 11 taels, new goods were 11 taels and 2 qian, and No. 8 Dutch red was 9 taels and 4 qian. The trend is generally stable. Taikoo Sugar B mark was 12 taels, DY mark was 11 taels and 8 qian, HX mark was 11 taels, 7 qian and 7.5 fen to 7 qian, HM mark was 11 taels, 4 qian and 2.5 fen. Demand is not strong, and the market is also weak and lacks vitality. Dumped coarse sand white is falling more and more. Sassoon's bag was 5 yuan, 7 jiao and 8 fen, with no interest at all. Huaxin's bag price for shipments in October and November was 5 yuan and 7 jiao, with few recipients. The market sentiment is generally weak. The Hao Pan had Zhenxiang Hao selling thousands of bags of Hong Kong transportation goods, with Dutch red priced at 9 taels and 4 qian. At the same time, Huaxin sold more than a thousand bags of raw rice goods, priced at 9 taels and 5 qian. The market is still firm.

Silk and Tea, Double Palace Cocoon Goods are Scarce and Prices are High 125

▲ The cost of silk requires more than 600 taels... All five silk factories have resumed operations. Five local Double Palace silk factories had previously reduced their machines and suspended operations due to sluggish silk sales, high raw material prices, and heavy losses. After the new cocoons were listed, only three Double Palace silk factories started work. Now that the silk industry public bonds have begun to be issued, the Double Palace silk factories can also enjoy the rights of public bonds. Therefore, the two factories that have suspended work have now also received public bonds and started machines to work. Double Palace cocoon goods are scarce and sales are smooth, and the quoted price is rising. Each 100 jin of silk costs 640 taels, plus reeling labor, etc., and the cost of silk requires more than 800 taels.

Local News

Last Night at Shihudang Station 146

Military Train and Passenger Train Collide

More Than Ten Injured on Each Side

Vehicles Not Seriously Damaged

At Shihudang Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, at around 7:30 last night, the Beijing-Hangzhou express train and a military train collided. More than ten passengers and soldiers were injured. Rescue vehicles were dispatched for repairs, and traffic is expected to be restored. The long-distance telephone line on that route was damaged at around 7:00 beforehand, so details could not be fully ascertained. The details of the collision are recorded as follows:

▲Military Train Departure The 2nd Division, 4th Brigade, 7th Regiment of the Shangxing Bridge Garrison Army, was ordered to defend the Songhu area. They requested three trains from the Railway Bureau to be sent to the South Bridge Station for use. After the Railway Bureau prepared them, they were dispatched in three special trains yesterday. The first train, with 24 cars, carried the first battalion of the regiment, departing at 10:00 am to Longhua. The second train, with 26 cars, carried the second battalion, departing at 12:40 pm to the North Station. The third train, with 25 cars, carried the entire third battalion, departing at 2:00 pm, heading directly to Wusong to disembark and garrison.

▲Express Train Also Arrives When the third military train arrived at Shihudang Station at around 7:30 last night, the 32nd Beijing-Hangzhou express train from Shanghai to Hangzhou also arrived at the station to exchange trains.

▲Usual Train Operation According to the usual train operation of that route, when two trains arrive at the station at the same time to exchange trains, the train that arrives first can proceed directly to the platform and park properly. Then, the other train is allowed to enter the station. Whether or not a train can enter the station is based on whether the flag is lowered or not.

▲Collision Situation At around 7:30 last night, the third military train entered the station first. According to regulations, the head of the 32nd Beijing-Hangzhou express train waited outside with the flag raised, waiting for the military train to park properly at the platform. Only after seeing the flag lowered could it enter. Unexpectedly, last night, the 32nd Beijing-Hangzhou express train, without waiting for the flag to be lowered, proceeded directly to the platform, entering the same track at the same time. With a loud bang, they collided. Fortunately, both sides were moving slowly, and no major danger was caused.

▲Locomotive Damaged After the trains collided, the iron on the front of the train was damaged. The hooks of each car were also not seriously damaged. After the damage to the locomotive, etc., is slightly repaired, it can restore its original condition.

▲Rescue Train Dispatched After receiving the news from the North Station, the responsible personnel of several departments discussed and decided to dispatch a rescue train from the North Station to make repairs, so that normal operation could be restored. The rescue train departed from the North Station at 11:05 pm, heading directly to Shihudang.

▲Passengers and Soldiers Injured After the two trains collided, more than ten passengers and soldiers in the trains suffered minor injuries. None were in life-threatening condition. After doctors provided some bandages, they could leave the station.

Navigation News During the Flood 147

▲Refugee Epidemic Prevention Inoculation This time, the Yangtze River ports suffered severe floods. Many disaster victims from Hankou and Wuhu have come to Shanghai. Wherever there is a major flood, there is bound to be an epidemic, because the water is dirty and easily breeds epidemics. The Harbor Quarantine Office has decided to implement vaccinations for disaster victims when they disembark from ships in Hankou and Wuhu. When each ship arrives in Shanghai, it will also be inspected, starting from the 4th of this month.

▲Japanese Rescue Overseas Merchants There are many Japanese in various ports along the Yangtze River. After the flood occurred this year, the Japanese in Shanghai formed a flood relief team of the Tongren Association. They have requested the Nisshin Steamship Company of this port to send the Xiangjiang Maru, carrying 10 doctors, 7 clerks, 16 nurses, and 6 employees, a total of more than 40 people. They have prepared medicines in Shanghai and set off for Wuhu, Hankou, Changsha, and other places to rescue Japanese people.

▲Hunan Goods Expedited for Export Many European and American countries purchase minerals and tung oil from Hunan Province, and sesame from Yichang and Shashi, for export. Usually, these goods are transported from Hunan to Hankou, and then transferred to Shanghai for export. Recently, the warehouses in Hankou have been submerged in water. The goods cannot be unloaded upon arrival in Hankou. So, the Hunan merchants telegraphed Shanghai, requesting that these goods be transported directly to Shanghai for export and requesting expedited loading. Therefore, Taikoo and Jardine Matheson have added Hunan route ships to transport Hunan cargo to Shanghai, without stopping in Hankou, and then transferring to Jiang ships to Shanghai. The American merchants in Shanghai have already loaded the purchased minerals for export. The first batch has arrived in recent days and is being declared for export, it is said.

Japanese Emperor's Relief Fund Arrives in Shanghai 148

Yesterday, the Japanese Consulate Delivered the Disaster Relief Fund

Equivalent to More Than 226,000 Chinese Dollars

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, it was rumored that the Japanese Showa Emperor generously donated 100,000 Japanese yen to China for flood relief and had already sent it to Song Ziwen, Chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee of the National Government, last time. This is not true. According to sources at the Japanese Consulate General in this port, the funds were only delivered yesterday (2nd) morning at 10:00 am by Mr. Okazaki, secretary of the embassy, with a handwritten letter from Minister Chongguang to Chairman Song, and a Yokohama Specie Bank draft, to the secretariat of the Disaster Relief Committee of the National Government at 1 Jiujiang Road for collection. Based on yesterday's market price of Japanese yen, the equivalent in Chinese currency was 226,950 yuan, it is said.

Disaster Relief News from Various Provinces Yesterday 149

Key News from the National Government's Disaster Relief Committee

Donation Report The Finance Group of the National Government's Disaster Relief Committee released a report yesterday on the donations received from all parties since its establishment up to yesterday (2nd). The donations include 100,000 Japanese yen, equivalent to 226,950 Chinese dollars; 100,000 yuan from the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau and armories; 100,000 yuan from the Central Bank; 100,000 yuan from the Bank of China; 80,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications; 50,000 yuan from the National Commercial Bank; 50,000 yuan from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; 50,000 yuan from the postal bureau, the postal savings bureau, the postal workers' union, and postal employees; 50,000 yuan from the British American Tobacco Company; 50,000 yuan from Caisse Duvres Derst Phblic; 25,000 yuan from the Shanghai Bank; 25,000 yuan from the International Savings Society; 5,000 yuan from the staff of Sincere Company; 10,000 yuan from Sincere Company; 20,000 yuan from Wing On Company; 100,000 yuan from Sir Robert Ho Tung; In addition, there are many donations of less than 10,000 yuan down to 1 yuan. In total, donations of 1,044,580 yuan and 6 cents, and 6,179,491 taels of silver were received. (Xinsheng News Agency)

▲Soliciting Clothing and Bedding Yesterday, the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, based on a telegram from a special commissioner sent to Wuhan to investigate the disaster, said that the weather upstream had suddenly turned cold and the disaster victims were shivering from the cold, which was unbearable to witness. Chairman Song immediately appointed Huang Renlin to handle the solicitation of clothing and bedding to be transported to the disaster area. It is reported that Huang Renlin has begun planning after receiving the order. The general plan is as follows: (1) Send letters to chambers of commerce, charitable organizations, and church organizations to solicit donations on their behalf; (2) Solicit items such as clothing, trousers, shoes, hats, quilts, mattresses, etc., anything that can keep warm is included in the solicitation; (3) After collection, inspection will be carried out: A. Disinfection B. Washing C. Mending D. Sorting; (4) The organization or individual that solicits the most donations will be praised and rewarded by the committee. It is also heard that the official letters to be sent to each organization to serve as collection points will be issued tomorrow.

Telegram from Cheng Jingsheng from Zhenjiang 150

Addressed to the following esteemed gentlemen: Chairman Zhu of the National Government Relief Committee Working Group, Chairman Xu of the Committee, Standing Committee Members of the Emergency Relief Committee Yu, Wang, Zhang, and Wu, and Gentlemen of the Suzhou Relief Committee Wang, Huang, Wen, Wu, and Lu: Telegram number 30 has been sent. This morning, I departed with Chairman Ye, Director Li, and Xia Feng towards Yang, to meet with Song Qiao and Xiao Gu to discuss the establishment of refugee camps. The number of disaster victims flocking to the Gao Shao refugee camps is extremely high, and the three camps are insufficient, so additional camps have been set up. At noon, we arrived at Shao. The water level has dropped by more than ten feet, and the embankment walls have been completely submerged in the entire town. Not a single roof can be seen. At that time, more than 20,000 people were adrift in the river. The houses on the embankment are dilapidated, and the disaster victims are gathered together. Food is being sent daily from the Yang camps. Beyond the exposed Jin and western embankments, it is a vast expanse of water. More than 3,000 disaster victims from the Fifth District are still sleeping in the open. The waters are treacherous and ferries cannot land. We are hiring small boats to circumnavigate the lake to provide relief and send people to the Yang refugee camps. We then arrived outside Youcheng. More than 10,000 households in the town have been washed away without a trace. Only the treetops are swaying above the towering white waves. Inside the city, the water is chest-deep, and rescue boats are frequently going back and forth. The south of the city is safe and is a gathering place for disaster victims. Refugees have already been received from rooftops and treetops during sunny days, and a retreat to Yang has been opened. However, between the protective embankments, corpses are everywhere, and the stench is unbearable. It is a tragic sight to behold. There are eleven major breaches, ranging in width from dozens of feet to one hundred sixty or seventy feet. The water is raging fiercely and is expanding daily. According to Xia Feng Shu Xiang, it is currently impossible to obtain soil to plug the breaches, and it is inevitable that the three lakes will shift eastward. Ferries to various villages are impassable. Public announcements have been made to civilian boats to rescue disaster victims and send them to various camps along the way, with each person receiving five dimes per ocean dollar. Thirty relief workers have been assigned to carry food for distribution. Currently, the waters of Taidongxing are rising. More than 10,000 households in the three towns of Shibao, Gao West Village, Song Guo, and Zhu Qiao have been completely swept away by the lake waves. The dilapidated houses are all in the water, with only black shadows remaining. Post-disaster recovery efforts at various breaches are being discussed by Chairman Ye and Mr. Wang Wu. The most urgent need is to immediately transport 500 shi of coarse rice and 10,000 bags of wheat flour to be distributed by the Zhen authorities under the control of Jing. The number of disaster victims being rescued will inevitably be large. The Yang and Zhen refugee camps are insufficient, so please prepare in Shanghai. More details to follow. Cheng Jingsheng bows. East.

Emergency Relief Committee Held Standing Committee Meeting Yesterday 151

The Shanghai Emergency Relief Committee for the Water Disaster held its fifth standing committee meeting yesterday. Attendees included Xu Shiying, Zhu Qinglan, Wang Yiting, Wen Lanting, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Wu Zhihao, Qu Wenliu, and Li Zuyu. The following items were reported: (1) Since August 26, 28 letters requesting disaster relief have been received from various provinces, including 13 from Anhui, 11 from Jiangsu, 2 from Henan, and 2 from Hunan. (2) From August 7 to September 1, the committee received a total of 362,809.17 ocean dollars in relief funds, as well as 200 taels of silver and 72 additional ocean dollars. Total expenditures amounted to 147,122.74 ocean dollars. (3) The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang sent a letter notifying the committee that it had organized a disaster relief fundraising team of party members to collect funds and remit them to the committee for distribution, and requested 250 donation booklets. (4) The Shanghai Disaster Victim Reception Office informed that it would be formally established on September 1 at the Rengu Public Office, Dadongmen, Nanshi. Items for discussion: (1) Mr. Zhang Junjie submitted 10,000 ocean dollars raised by the Buddhist layman Jue Mi for Mrs. Hardoon to provide relief for the water disaster in Jiangbei. According to Mr. Zhang's suggestion, it is proposed that the committee purchase flour on its behalf for distribution in the disaster area. How should this be handled? Please discuss. (2) The Citizens' Federation organized a water disaster appeal team and encountered difficulties in refusing donations along the way. Please prepare two donation barrels and send personnel from the committee to be responsible for handling the case. Should this be discussed? (3) The Shanghai Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association sent a letter stating that the 12th Standing Committee meeting resolved to confiscate Japanese goods and allocate all proceeds to disaster relief. Please send personnel from the committee to make contact. (4) The Anti-Japanese Association sent a letter stating that confiscated Japanese yarn should be used entirely for disaster relief. Please send personnel from the committee to make contact. Please discuss the above two items together. (5) A joint letter from the five merchants, Zhisheng and others, proposed to quickly set up fundraising booths in major commercial areas or shops at intersections. (6) Committee member Wang Xiaoyu submitted an unsigned letter containing opinions on disaster relief donation booths. (7) Mr. Luo Zhongyan submitted a letter outlining his thoughts on disaster relief fundraising. (8) Mr. Tang Wenzhi submitted a letter outlining proposals for emergency water disaster relief. Discuss the above three items together. (9) Anhui women request funds for women's shelters. (10) The organization and liaison of various groups. (11) Disaster relief distribution in Hunan, Hubei, Henan, and Jiangxi. (12) Should relief funds continue to be collected before distribution? (Resolution) Distribute by province: 10,000 ocean dollars each for Henan, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Guizhou, 20,000 ocean dollars for Guangdong, 1,500 bags of rice (approximately worth 30,000 ocean dollars) and 10,000 ocean dollars worth of wheat flour for Zhejiang (allocated in rice), 2,000 bags of rice for Jiangsu, 1,000 bags of rice for Anhui, 12,000 ocean dollars for southern Anhui, 5,000 ocean dollars for Hefei, and 3,000 ocean dollars for the Wuhu women's shelter. (13) Discussion of detailed operational rules. (Resolution) Standing Committee Member Xu Shiying will revise and implement them. (14) The committee's budget for expenses and personnel, and the request for additional personnel to assist. (Resolution) To be handled by the Standing Committee. (15) Additional Executive Committee members were recommended. (Resolution) Cha Liangzhao, Yao Wugang, Yu Yefeng, Mao Benfeng, You Jusun, Chen Bogang, and Qian Zhixiang were added as Executive Committee members, with Chen Bogang as the Director of the Transportation Group and Cha Liangzhao as a member of the Relief Affairs Group. (16) Matters submitted to the committee: (A) Send a telegram to the Legislative Yuan supporting the passage of the 80 million yuan relief bond issuance. (Resolution) Postpone sending for two days. (B) Cigarette tax increase. (Resolution) Send a telegram to the National Government to implement it. (C) Nomination of a Secretary-General. Secretary-General Wen Lanting and Qu Wenliu simultaneously resigned. (Resolution) Wu Zhihao was nominated to take the position. (D) Nomination of a Director of the General Affairs Group. Jin Guanfu stated that he was already the Secretary of the Relief Committee and was also helping in the National Government Relief Committee's disaster area working group. It was difficult to oversee the General Affairs Group as well. It was resolved that Standing Committee Member Qu Wenliu would take on the role of Director of the General Affairs Group, and Jin Guanfu would still serve as Deputy Director. Jin initially declined, but after much persuasion, he agreed to do his best and fulfill his obligations.

Ning Shao Emergency Relief Association for the Hankou Disaster Held a General Meeting Yesterday 152

The Ning Shao Emergency Relief Association for the Hankou Disaster convened a temporary emergency meeting at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association yesterday at 4:00 PM. More than 50 people attended, including Yu Qiaqing, Xu Qianlin, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Xiaoyu, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Yansong, Lou Xunru, Sun Meitang, Zhang Jiguang, Yan Chengde, Ge Yucheng, Lu Zhinan, and Yu Futian. Fang Jiaobo was elected as chairman. The meeting reported on the recent water disaster in Hankou and the situation of the relief team sent by the association to Hankou, which had returned to Shanghai. Representative Hong Xuefan stood up and briefly stated that the team departed on the 22nd and arrived in Hankou on the afternoon of the 25th. Small boats were dispatched to rescue fellow villagers in various parts of Hankou. The first trip of the "Xin Ning Xing" carried more than 1,500 disaster-stricken fellow villagers. The second trip of the "Yong Xing" carried more than 400 fellow villagers. Because most of the fellow villagers on the ships wanted to return to their hometowns, the "Yong Xing" was sent directly to Ningbo. All the staff of the team, except for a few who remained in Hankou, returned with the ship. The detailed situation has already been reported to the association via letters and telegrams from time to time, so I will not elaborate further. Next, Director Mao Heyuan reported on the accounting situation, briefly stating that the total amount of cash brought by the team to Hankou was 2,000 ocean dollars, specifically for use on the ship and for temporary relief. The current expenditures include 660 ocean dollars for rice, over 350 ocean dollars for tea and labor on the "Xin Ning Xing," over 300 ocean dollars for food and other expenses on the "Yong Xing," and over 370 ocean dollars for travel expenses for the staff on the "Longhe" and "Shangchuan" (Director Mao Heyuan, Doctor Xing Xuefan, and Xie Qigang paid for their own boat tickets, alcohol, and other expenses and did not claim any expenses from the association). Other miscellaneous expenses are listed in a detailed bill, which was prepared and reported by Chen Yuansheng, the accountant sent by the accounting committee member Lou Xunru, and can be verified. As for the food prepared by the director, it was brought in large quantities, including cigarettes and alcohol, because the stay in Hankou was uncertain, also to prevent the spread of disease. It has now been decided that Mao Heyuan, Hong Xuefan, and Xie Qigang will pay for these food items themselves to avoid external criticism. Next, Doctor Xie Qigang reported that one-third of the fellow villagers in Hankou were ill, and there would inevitably be a major epidemic after the flood. A preventive hospital should be established as soon as possible. Zhang Shenzhi then reported that fellow villagers in Hankou had already organized preparations for a preventive hospital through the Hubei Fellow Villagers Association, but funding was needed from the association. It was resolved that the association would subsidize 10,000 ocean dollars. Finally, the chairman proposed that the ship rental from the Sanbei Company be paid at 80% of the actual cost. The second proposal was to donate to the association. Finally, all the representatives present stood up to express their gratitude and condolences to Director Mao, Hong, Xie, and the staff of the relief team to Hankou. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Appeal from the Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association 153

The Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai received a telegram from County Magistrate Du of Yancheng yesterday. Yancheng is located downstream of the Huaiyun River. Since the opening of the three dams, including Cheluo, the water has flowed straight down, and the entire territory has become a swamp. On August 25, the postal Shao Yun embankment suddenly collapsed again, pouring down and flowing eastward. In the western corner, the submerged fields are more than seven or eight feet deep. Even those with dikes to defend were mostly destroyed. Young people clung to trees waiting for rescue, and most of the women and children drowned. Houses were gone, and cooking was impossible. The scene was heartbreaking and unbearable. After learning this, the Fellow Villagers Association, in addition to rushing to raise emergency relief, has requested the provincial government and the Shanghai Water Disaster Relief Committee to send personnel to investigate and provide assistance. It has also sent a telegram requesting the Jiangbei Water Conservancy Bureau to block the collapsed embankments of the Grand Canal to reduce the downward flow.

Representatives of the Hankou Water Disaster Emergency Relief Association Arrive in Shanghai

Yesterday, Zhu Huaibing, a member of the Hubei Provincial Government of the Hankou Water Disaster Emergency Relief Association, Kai Juntian, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, Zhou Xingtang, a representative of the Chamber of Commerce, Wang Yi, a representative of the Bankers Association, and other gentlemen arrived in Shanghai and stayed at No. 88 Yipinxiang. It is said that they are begging for relief for millions of disaster victims in Wuhan and have brought photos of the disaster situation on the ground. They plan to hold a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce to report and ask various institutions, groups, and businesses in Shanghai to unite to provide relief and blessings to the disaster victims. It is believed that people in Shanghai are happiest when doing good deeds and will provide as much help as possible.

Disaster Relief Work of the Sino-Foreign Charity Relief Association 154

▲Loading Flour for Emergency Relief to Hankou The Sino-Foreign Charity Relief Association, due to the lack of food for the disaster victims in Hankou, specially went to the Fufeng Flour Factory yesterday to pick up 500 bags of flour and handed them over to the Longhe vessel to be released in Hankou. Father Rao Jiaju, a Western member of the association, had already set off for Hankou and is expected to arrive on the 2nd. Father Rao will then find ways to distribute it. ▲The Jiangxin Ship Carried Refugees to Shanghai Yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangxin ship arrived in Shanghai from Hankou. In addition to passengers, it carried more than 300 disaster victims. According to the ship's staff, the ship carried more than 800 disaster victims when it left port, all from Hubei, Mianyang, Hankou, Hunan, Anhui, and other places. The ship stopped to load and unload cargo along the way, and some disaster victims disembarked at various ports. It is estimated that 100 people disembarked at Jiujiang, Anqing was not allowed to board or disembark, 200 people disembarked at Datong, and about 300 people disembarked at Nanjing, so that only more than 300 people arrived in Shanghai. Most of them were poor people fleeing the disaster. Except for a small number who came to Shanghai to seek refuge with relatives and friends, the remaining 200 people were taken in by the Social Affairs Bureau, together with the Disaster Relief Association, and housed in the Zhabei refugee camp.

Feng Jishan Hall's Grand Vision of Donating Rent 155

Feng Jishan Hall sent a letter to the Emergency Relief Committee, stating: "Dear Sirs, the continuous rain this summer has caused a disaster unprecedented in a century. According to newspaper reports, the disaster area covers as much as 1.5 million square miles, and the number of disaster victims, in Wuhan alone, is as many as 300,000. If we combine the disaster areas of 16 provinces, it is probably no less than 50 to 60 million. Houses have been washed away, and fields have been completely destroyed. The vast calamity is a terrible blow. All those who are human should follow the teachings of universal love and contribute generously to overcome this crisis. The managers of our hall, considering the severity of the disaster and the urgent needs of the disaster victims, believe that all people in the country must follow the example of those who have been entrusted with great responsibilities and actively contribute to overcome the crisis. Therefore, the hall has been instructed to set a plan to donate the rent collected for the entire year after deducting expenses. The entire rent for the first month (starting from July of this year) will be donated. For the second month to the twelfth month, 5% of the rent collected will be donated as a relief fund. The total amount of the donation for the entire year has been calculated to be 1,501 taels, 5 mace and 5 fen of silver (equivalent to 2,068 ocean dollars and 25 cents). A check for this amount is being sent. We hope that you will accept it on our behalf for disaster relief. This small contribution is not enough to save the burning cart of wood, but we hope that benevolent gentlemen will make a grand vision and contribute from the income of their properties and lands, either according to the plan we have proposed or by proposing other plans, all are acceptable. If the property still has mortgages or other loan relationships, it may be possible to first deduct the interest on the mortgage or other loans, and then donate as much as possible, regardless of the amount. In short, this matter should be initiated from the heart, without waiting for others to solicit donations. The entire country should unite to overcome this national crisis, in order to open a path to life for tens of millions of disaster victims. Otherwise, the number of disaster victims is so large, they are already without food or clothing, waiting to die. What can they not do? Once they take the risk, not only will social order and human peace be impossible to maintain, but also the economy and property of areas not affected by the disaster will be destroyed. In the past, the great rebellions at the end of the Sui and Yuan dynasties all started with the people living in misery, and the bandits of the late Ming dynasty ravaged the whole world. It all started with seeing the disaster and not helping, until resentment accumulated and exploded. It was too late to regret. The rich and noble, especially those with large properties, suffered the most from looting. Similar mistakes are repeated, and history is full of such examples. Moreover, the value of property depends on the regulation of consumption and production to maintain balance. Now, the production side has been lost due to the displacement of tens of millions of people, and the consumption side has increased as a result. Will the country's economy not fall into a state of collapse? What value can property have? Therefore, today's matter is actually saving oneself while saving others. It is directly saving people's lives and indirectly protecting one's own property. It is impossible not to think deeply about it. Furthermore, since the 19th century, science has flourished, with a progress that can be measured in leaps and bounds. Its contribution to mankind is immense, but there is still no way to avoid the spread of natural disasters. This is not only true for our country, but also for European and American countries. For example, the earthquake in Italy last year, the snowstorm in England this year, the drought in the United States, and the great earthquake in Japan in previous years, all cannot be stopped by science. This is not the fault of science itself, but mankind, having trusted in the omnipotence of science, cannot help but harbor doubts about religion, or even slander various religions, wanting to destroy them all at once. How can we know that we will not offend Heaven and bring about disasters? Moreover, even with science, pushing its omnipotence, the use of electricity, air, and Feng Shui is also inexhaustible. Having taken what is inexhaustible, how can we know that we will not change the climate of nature directly and indirectly, brewing various disasters? Therefore, although science is omnipotent, it can never control this nature. Since it cannot control this nature, it cannot but have a devout belief in this nature. This is the meaning of the saying "Heaven protects" in our Confucianism. Now that disasters are coming, and the people are not living well, it is important to raise funds for relief. After the pain has subsided, we should all rise up with faith to meet the blessings of Heaven. All those who are saving people and those who are suffering from the disaster should have this awareness and not say that the matter involves superstition and can be rejected. This is the foolish opinion of our humble selves, which cannot be avoided in words, and is hoped to be enlightened by all gentlemen. The above is all the intention of the manager of our hall, who instructed us to convey it, and did not want to come forward in his own name, so we avoid it. Our hall is called Jishan Hall, which takes the meaning of accumulating good deeds. It is not a charity organization, but only an office for managing ordinary real estate. We hereby declare this together. We respectfully ask for your understanding. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Emergency Relief Committee for the Water Disaster in Various Provinces, Feng Jishan Hall respectfully, August 29, 20th year.
